<userid>111596375275821447947</userid>< Pics>
None</Pics>
< Text>
I've been to Which Wich a few times now (at a few different locations), and I must say it's definitely my new go-to sandwich place for SoCal (I don't think it has expanded much further, but I may be wrong).

Let me be clear. Starting about two years ago, I was the biggest fan of Subway sandwiches. I wanted nothing more than a lifetime supply of the stuff. Then I researched a little and found out about the crap they put in their sandwiches, and that was the last I heard of Subway.

Along came Which Wich, and first and foremost is the sheer variety of options they have for sandwiches. CLEARLY outnumbering Subway by a long shot, Which Wich gives you a number of options for each type of meat (or vege, or breakfast, etc.).

I've never been unsatisfied with the sandwiches I get here, and their system is actually pretty unique. You take the apt bag for the type of sandwich you want and check off the ingredients you like. Give it, pay for it, and get it within 5 min (obviously longer if busier). DEFINITELY cheaper than Subway, so honestly the best option in my opinion.</Text>
